spyan snga bkra shis rnam rgyal de dag snang can zhig yod 'dug pas mjal gleng dang phan tshun du chos kyi 'brel pa gsan res mdzad /
mchod mjal skabs su 'dra rin po ches /
skyes bu dam pa byon pa legs /
dad pa'i sa gzhi gang pa legs /
phrag dog rlung dmar zhi ba legs /
gdul bya smin grol bkod ba legs /
zhes gsung byon /
der 'khod pa'i skya ser rnams kyi don rgya chen po mdzad bzhin pa'i ngang nas mal gro brgyud de 'bras spungs su phebs /
rje rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa da nyid /
rgyal nas tshur phebs ba'i lam kha phan bde dgon par sku mya ngan las bzla ba'i tshul bstan /
de yang zhal chems su /
nged kyi skye ba dwags po bla mngar 'ong bas /
der nyer len gnang ba zhu zhes pa'i zhu 'phrin 'jog par mdzad pa ltar /
sprul pa'i sku mthu stobs nus pa'i bdag nyid chen po de byon /
'bras spungs su gnas tshul gsan pa dang dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i thabs rgya cher mdzad /
dgun chos la rje gong ma'i gsung 'bum gyi 'phro mus gnang /
sa rta'i lo gsar smon lam chen mo sogs grub rjes /
'bras spungs su tshogs chen la sgrub thabs rgya mtsho rdzogs par gnang /
mgon po zhal gyi bsnyen ba zhig mdzad /
de skabs yar glungs bkra shis bde legs su 'ol kha nas lung bstan zhus pa'i yi ge ngo bo las /
sa pho rta lo hor zla gnyis pa'i tshes nyer gcig gi nyin /
dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i drung du /
sde pa 'ol kha stag rtse bas lung bstan zhus pa la /
zhabs drung rin po ches mchog gi sprul sku thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku cha bzang po zhus pa'i len ni / /
mnyam med thub pa'i dbang po dang / /
rang gang mos dpal ldan bla ma sogs / /
yi dam mthu ldan srung ma mchod / /
rnal 'byor rgyu lus shel dkar mchod rten yang / /
glo bur 'jig par ma gyur kyang / /
mi gtsang 'khon grib la brten pa'i / /
nad kyi dri nogs phra mo 'khor / /
gting nas bar chad cher med kyang / /
gnas skabs rnal 'byor rang gi snang ba lam du long / /
yi dam lha yi bsnyen sgrub 'bad pa thon lan med kyi sbyin gtong kun la 'bad / /
rigs drug gi sems can kun rnams skyong / /
de khas bar chad kyi rigs rnams sel 'gyur zhing / /
'khor 'das gnyis kye dbus su ni / /
rnal 'byor rigs ldan rgyu lus shel dkar tshugs / /
rtsa ba ba gam brtan gyur cing / /
dbus kyi bum pa bar snang yongs la khyab / /
rtse mo chos 'khor gser gyi gser phru de / /
steng dga' ldan lha gnas yul du khyab / /
mi gtsang 'khon grib kun la phyogs bzhir gzur / /
gtum chen khro bo nga bran 'khor bcas gnas pa'i sar / /
mchod gtor spyan gzigs nam mkha' gang ba shoms / /
'phrin las kyi sgo mo phyogs bzhir kho bos 'byed / /
rnal 'byor da lta gnas pa'i yul phyogs der / /
dgos med kyi 'khrug long slong gyur pas / /
sa de nas nyi ma nub phyogs ri sna yi / /
lung gsum mdo ru khrag gi mtsho mo 'khyil / /
dgos med kyi kha mchu mang po 'byung rigs drug gi sems can snying rje chen pos skyongs / /
dge ba nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam par 'gyur / /
legs bshad kyi go yul de la 'tshol / /
zhes lung bstan to / /
drung nas rin po che'i sku cha zhus pa'i lan du /
rang mos bla ma ya ngam gus pas mchod / /
rgyu lus thang @# / /
shing rdong chen de / /
lo yi bskal ba cung zad bgrangs byung bas / /
gnas ya mtshan can gyi rten rnams la /
phyag mchod skor ba 'bum gter dang / /
lan med kyi sbyin gtong kun la thong / /
mthar thug don gyi snying po la 'bad na / /
lo ni gnyis bcad gsum gyi ngo tsam du / /
rgyu lus srog gi sdong chen tshugs gyur cing / /
rtsa ba drod gsher bcud kyis 'tsho par 'gyur / /
legs bshad kyi go yul de la tshol / /
zhes pa byung 'dug go /
hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga'i gza' skar bzang ba la /
se ra theg chen gling gi chos kyi khril phebs glegs bam rin po che'i tshogs chos gnang /
lhar me tog gi char phab cing /
kun dad pa'i sa la bkod /
lugs gnyis kyi dga' ston rgya chen po bsgrubs so / /
rmad byung rnam dkar dkar po'i 'bras bu kun / /
gcig tu 'dzag byed byed po bla na med / /
phul byung 'phrin las las bzang mtha' klas pa / /
sngal mkhas bla ma la lus 'gro ba'i mgon / /
mgon khyod dkon cog 'bangs su gyur pa'i dus / /
dus gsum gsal ba'i lung bstan nyer bab de / /
de ltar dgongs nas lhun grub dga' ba'i tshal / /
chal chen spel ba'i sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs / /
theg chen chos tshul ma lus pa / /
theg gsum mthun mong ma yin pa'i / /
theg mchog la brtson gling gi khrir / /
theg kun ma 'dres mkhyan 'di mdzes / /
slar 'bras spungs su phebs /
rin po che kun bzang rtse ba la zhal gnad dbab kyi mgon po'i rjes gnang gsan /
de'i zhal thang hal tshon ma zhig 'phral bzhengs gnang /
tshal ba'i mgan po ko gtums ma dang 'dra ba zhig yong gsungs /
zhal khebs kyi mtha' skor mar btsams /
skabs shig kha bya bas sar drag dang thog 'khyug yong la khad ba lta bu'i 'tshub 'gyur byung /
da lta dga' ldan pho brang gi gzims chung mgon khang na bzhugs /
de skabs dga' ldan ba dpon blon gyis skyor mo lung chos sde la bskor rgyag byas pas /
phyi nang gnyis kar mi gron che ba sogs byung bar /
dpal mgon gyi lung bstan der dgongs te /
bar chings su phebs /
chos sdes dpang lag mdzad de phan tshun mtha' dag bde 'jags su grol /
slar 'bras spungs su phebs nas bzhugs thog /
hor dpon thar 'bum gyis sngar nas hor nang du phebs dgos pa'i gsol ba mang du btab cing /
'di res gdan 'dren pa yang slebs /
chibs kham sgyur ba'i sngon du| chos skyong chen po sku phebs nas hor rnams la 'di skad cas /
byang sha zan gyi rigs yin kyang /
dkar po dge ba'i blo skyes /
chos dang chos sma ba la dad pa thob nas sprul sku mthong ba don ldan lta bu'i bla ma spyan 'drongs pa 'di bsod nams chen po yin na / /
bka' gdabs pa bsam 'gal zhig /
ces gsangs so / /
rje'i drung la'ang 'di skad ces gsol te /
da lo skor tsam phebs ba de srog chags tshad med pa'i don chen por 'gyur bar 'dug /
'on kyang zhag nyi shu las mang ba ma bzhugs /
mi ngo rtags can zhig byungs na tshur spyon cig ces zhus ba / /
de yang gsal ba nan gyis btab par brtan rong bo 'dam du chibs kha bsgyur ba'i lam zhor du /
lha sar jo shAka mjal zhing smon lam gnang /
sgrol brgyud glang thang gi thang du phebs ban hor gyi gdan 'dren par nams rta rtsal '+k+ran pa sogs dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur stan sde pa dpon g.yog rnams kyi bsu ba'i bgod pa dang bcas o rgyan gshas kar phebs /
thams cad mkhyen ba pu ston rin po che'i chos kyi gdar khri la mngon bar 'jogs pa'i mkhar chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gsang chen slob bshad kyi bstan 'dzin chen po @# / /
mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug mtshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bzhugs pa dang 'grig /
dar dpon slob mjal 'dzom mdzad pas chos rje'i gsung las /
nga rje gong ma'i slob ma yin pas dal ma 'dir mjal ba 'di rten 'brel shin tu legs zhes bla ma'i rnal 'byor gya chos 'brel zhig zhus /
de nub mthar chen la /
gur gya mgon po'i rjes gnang zhig bsan /
dpon slob gnyis phan tshun du 'bel gtam gyis thugs dgyes par byung /
rim gyis 'ong 'jo'i mdor phebs pa'i che /
yul lugs kyi go khrab gyon pa'i hor gyi rta ba stong phrag gis bsu ba dang bcas te hor dpon gyis thog mar mjal bas dad pa gting nas rnyed dpon mo yo khom bza'i sgar gzhis ldan byung du phebs /
bsnyen bkur zhus /
stag lung chos rje khri gdan zur gyas ja 'dren dang 'bul ba mdzad /
de nas rim gyis mtsho slo gong du phebs /
dpon gyis 'di sa bkra shis pas chos 'brel gyi thog ma gnang dgos zhus pa ltar sang zhogs dbang gral bsgrigs ba dang nyi ma shar ba dus mnyam 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char sogs byung bas hor rnams kyis pi wang gi sgra las drangs pa'i bstod pa phul /
de nas dpon tshang du bar sngon la song /
dpon slob rnams rim bzhin phyin sa phebs pa'i lam du /
hor gyis bsgor ba'i ja pa rnams kyis spyan 'dren zhus /
de dag rnams la mi 'jigs pa'i spyin pa gnang bar zhal gyis bzhes nas dbugs dbyung ste 'dam gzhung du phebs /
dpon tshang gi gur dkar po'i nang du gdan drangs te bkur sti gya nom pa bstab /
sngon ko khyim pa ye shes bla ma'i dgon shul du bzhugs skar mdzad nas chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor /
phyin chad ja la pa'i 'grul rnams la gnod ba mi byed bar gdams te /
dpon g.yog thams cad kyis bas blangs /
hor sog gi mi glen zhing snying rje chung ba sha lpags la longs spyod pa srin po lta bu rnams kyang sdig spong dge ba sgrub pa la gzhol bar gyur /
de nas dpon mo dang sras blon po rnams kyis kyang so sor spyan drangs te mchod cing bsnyen bkur /
bla ma bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi dpon po blo bzang ba dpon slob kyis bsnyen bkur zhing bka' chos mang du zhus /
dgun gyi dus yin kyang /
'khyags rom rnams chung zhu zhing spang ljongs m+r+gad kyi gos gyon pa sogs dbyar gyi lang tshe la 'gran pas kun ya mtshan par byed /
hor stod pa khra rgyal 'bum dang karma dpal sgom sde nang chen pa sogs kyi zhu yig dang bcas te gus mchod lhur len byas /
da skabs nub gcig bzhugs me gnang sar bka' las /
'dir hor lo bco lnga tsam rta kha zin pa la ngo mtshar du 'dug ste /

yod de /
lo bcu gcig yan la /
gung drag gi sngags 'bum phrag nyis brgya /
lo bdun yan la tshe dpag med kyi sngags 'bum phrag bcu gsum /
gzhan yang dbyangs can ma'i bsnyen pa sa ya lnga /
skyabs 'gro 'bum phrag bzhi /
le bcu gsum pa la rgyal du ye shes khyung nag gi sngags 'bum phrag gcig /
da lo yang 'bras spungs su dmigs brtse ma 'bum phrag bzhi song gsungs nyin gcig bzhugs sgar nas lho phyogs kyi lung pa zhig la phebs pas /
chur lam chu la zheng chen po zhig la /
chibs pa drag tu bskul te mchongs pas /

yul @# / /
bsrung so sam mdzad 'dug kyang /
ngas byas pa yin /
bla ma sngon ma rnams kyis ma mdzad pa mang po zhig byed dgos 'ong ba 'dug /
gser la'i rong du rta khams bzang gis pha bong chen po gcig la mchongs pa dang /
rtsim thang du rta 'drogs nas gad g.yang gom ba bco lnga tsam zhig la mchongs kyang skyon ma byung ba ni dkon cog gi thugs rje yin /
da res kyi 'di nged rang gi rtsal yin /
da dung mchongs che ba gcig la sku rim pa'i gur sgo tsam du rgyag /
'di'i bar la gom pa nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam yod gsung pa bzhin gzhag pas byung /
dpon gyi nga karma pa dang lhag tu 'bri gung chos rje la dad po yod de /
da res tsam ma byung bdag gi skyabs gnas mthar thug khyed yin pas nga rang la sger du lhag pa'i lha zhig gnang ba dang /
dgon pa 'debs dgos ba'i zhu ba phul ba ltar /
mgon po zhal gyi rjes gnar gnang ba'i tshe 'tshub 'gyur gyi rnam pa dang dpon rang la mgon po'i sku'i mthong snang byung zer /
dgon pa'i sa dmigs der phyag nas 'thor bar mdzad /
nyer lnga zhig dang 'grig pas gling me sbar ba sogs lha mchod kyi srol btsugs /
rim gyis r+wa sgreng du phebs /
jo bo phying dkar ba dngos su bsu ba la 'ongs pa gzigs /
zhag bdun gyi ring skya ser gyi tshogs la bka' gdams glegs bam gyi dkon chog 'bangs kyi skyes rabs dang /
snying bo don gsum gsungs /
jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rjes thog drangs pa'i rten gsum rnams zhib par mjal /

'bras spungs su phebs /
grub chen dpal ldan rdo rje zhes 'ja' lus kyi sku brnyes pa de la /
gzims chung nyi 'od du bde mchog lu hi pa'i dbang gsan pas /
drung nas gsung rab bas kyang 'jabs nas zhu thub pas las dang skal bar ldan par lung bstan /
nam mkha' las gser gyi me tog yu ba can gsum tsam bab pas gcig dngul gdung rin po che'i gzungs bzhugs la yod 'dug /
grub chen rang gis slob dpon padma la dngos su gsan pa'i tshe dbang phul /
mnga' ris lha'i btsun pa bsod nams dpal bzang gis /

'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i chos bka' 'ga' zhig phul /
de yang rgyal dbang padma 'byung gnas kyi bka' sdod /
sde brgyad thams cad kyi yang rje /
dregs pa kun 'dus kyi rgyal po /

gnas skabs su yang /

chos skyong @# / /
chen po sku khog la zhugs nas byon te /

kun rdzob bde na par snang ba'i ngor /

padma 'byung ngas yin /
zangs mdog dbal gyi ri bo'i rtser mor padma 'od kyi gzhal yas khang na yod dus /
padma 'byung gnas kyi bka' bsgos te /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i dag ster la btang ba yin /
de yang sprul sku mthong pa don ldan gyis zhi rgyas kyi sgo nas bstan pa 'dzin skyong gi 'phrin las mdzad /
nga pe dkar rgyal pos dbang drag gi sgo nas de'i 'gal rkyen sel zhing /
mthun rkyen 'gugs ba'i 'phrin las bsgrub /
de ltar gnyis kas kyang bstan pa'i dag ster byed dgos rgyu yin pa dgongs su gsol /
khyad par du'ang padma 'byung gnas kyis nga'i zas skal du /
dgra po'i sha khrag srog dbugs phog /
las skal du bstan pa dang bstan 'dzin bsrung bar bskos pa yin pas /
sngar yang padma 'byung gnas kyi bka' las 'da' ma myong /

gsungs te /
'o na dbus su mthong ba don ldan gyi skus gnon mnyam gzhag mdzad pas rtso bo de'i bzhugs gnas thams cad me tog padma'i rang bzhin yin pa /

de yang padma re re'i ge sar gyi steng du /
sngon ji ltar sku bltams pa nas nya bar bzung ste /
dpe dkar rgyal po dang zhal 'jam mdzad pa lan gyi mdzad pa rnam thar re re bzhin bkod pa /
de'i smad kyi cha la gzhan yang 'di yin gyi ngas bzungs med pa'i dgon gnas kyi bkod pa rgya che la lags pa'i mdun du /
nges bzung med pa'i chos grwa chen po / /
der yang chos nyan gyi dge 'dun tshogs pa chen pos yongs su bskor ba'i dbus su chos 'chad po chos ston gyi phyag rgya can /
thams cad kyang bkod pa chi mdzes /
de'i 'og tu nga pe dkar rgyal po khog pa la zhugs pa'i cha lugs thams cad da lta'i 'di ka 'dra ba la /
ru 'dren sde bzhi sku'i skyo rogs la sogs pa'i 'khor gyis bskor ba /

nga'i sprul pa yang sprul gyi mtha' /

yang dus re zhig na /
chos skyong gi zhal nas sprul sku 'phrang kha ba la 'di skad gsungs te /

de yang gar 'gro mi shes bas / /

sprul sku 'phrang kha ba dpal ldan blo bros bzang po zhes bas /

da nas sa gzhi'i dbang phyug gong mchen po dpal ngag gi dbang phyug bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po kwan ding ta'i bu shri hwong hang gis gser yig ba mngags te ti shrir bkur ba'i bka' shog stsal bar /

'bul ba gnang nas /

theg mar 'phyos su phebs /

'dod chos kyang thugs dgangs rdzags bar gnang /
de nas nang so 'phyong rgyas pas thob rgyal lha rtse dang /
srong btsan gzhis kar spyan drangs /

de nas mkhar thog tu phebs /

sgrol dkar gyi tshe dbang gnang /

de yang bka' las /
rtse zhabs drung dang mdzal rgyu'i de nub /

sbro zhing yangs pa cig gi dkyil du bzhugs 'dug pa la /
ri zhig gi rtse nas sbrin shin tu dkar ba cig dbu'i thang du nar gyis byung ba'i dkyil na mid kar po zhag gis 'o ma'i chu zhig dbu la blug byung ba dang /
thugs la 'di ci byed pa yin snyam tsan /
lha'i bu gos dkar po gyon pa zhig byung nas /
me tog gi 'phreng ba zhig sku pang du bskyur byung bas /

sku lus bde bas gang byung ba'i tshul /
sang nga sku zhabs su slebs dus bka' phebs gnang byung /

slar yang sgrol dkar sbyan bdun ma'i tshe dbang zag mo rgyas par 'bul ba gnang ba'i tshe /

tshe rim lhag ma rnams kyang phyag tu bzhes /

deng phyin chad nas ded mi ngo dang bcas pa la phyas 'tshal mi dgos zhes bkas bcad /

sa dbang phag mo @# / /

spyan snga chos grags pa gsung la /
dga' ldan chos 'byung du /
phag mo gru pa'i sde srid dang rgyal ba btsong kha pa'i bstan pa gnyis srog gcig lta bur 'dug gsung bas /
spyi sgos tshang ma'i sar dpal phag mo gru pa'i bstan pa 'di rgyas pa zhig dgos rgyur 'dug na'ang /

mdo sde mchod pa dang 'grig /

sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rnams la gus pa'i rnam 'gyur mdzad pa rang zhig yod 'dug cing /
'bri gung zhabs drung rin cen phun tshogs yab sras dang /
gzhan yang gsang sngags rnying ma'i rig sngags 'chang ba rnams la /
ayon rin po ches dam la btags pa'i sngon gyi tha tshig rjes su dran pa dang /

gzhan du na kar 'brug sprul sku /
stag lung chos rje sogs bod 'di'i rang gzhan gyi 'gro ba'i 'dren pa chen por grags pa phal che ba la dngos su thugs sun phyung ba dang /

der bzhugs /
de'i tshe sku zhang rin po che kun bzang rtse pa chos kyi dbang phyug ces /

nub cig bdag gi rmi lam na ye bzang rtser phyin pas /
de na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs sku tshad che gzhig bzhugs pa'i g.yas na mgon po tshe dpag med kyi sku dang /
ayon rin po che padma 'byung gnas kyi sku gnyis bzhugs shing /
gzhan yang rten gsum ngo shes ba dang mi shes pa mang po bzhugs pa'i drung na /

sku @# / /
gzhogs g.yas na rten mchod mang po 'dug pa'i khrod na rgyal ba tshe dpag med mgon bya sku bzhugs /
ayon rin po che'i rnam thar thang kha zhig kyang 'dug pas /
bzhugs tshul ngang bkod pa thams cad rmi lam dang mthun pa byung gsung /
rin po che pa de zhabs drung rin po che bsod nams rgya mtsho la spyan ras gzigs dngos kyi mos pa gnang ba yin /

'di skad ces /
'bi gung pa dang sgam po pa sogs 'gro ba thams cad dbang du 'du ba zhig e bzhed /

rang don du 'dod pa che ba la dga' ba med pas mi 'dod gsungs /
re zhig de khar sku mtshams mdzad pa'i mu nas /

rnga chings sogs 'khrid par mdzad de phyag len du thabs pa gnang /
de nas rgyal du bla ma chos mdzad pa dpon slob kyis gdan drangs /
gzims khang gong du rje rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa'i sku gdung zhugs la phul /
dbu thod dang zhal sgo sogs lha sku ring bsrel mang du byon ba'i rnyen ngo mtshar che ba rnams bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung gsar du bzhengs nas byams khang zhal ras lha khang du bzhugs su gsol /

drag po zhes pa lcags sgrel gyi lo gsar gnang /

de'i tshe yang sngar gyi mkha' 'gro ma de byung nas /

de la sngar zhus de ltar thugs la e bzhed /

de bas na da lta nas rten 'brel bsgrigs na legs /

de na re /

rim gyis 'bras spungs su phebs /

khro bo zhes ba shing glang gi lo gsar dang smon lam grub rjes /
zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin /

dus 'khor bsdus rgyud dang brgyad stong pa'i gsung sgrog /

gzhis ka snel bar byung ba /

grub @# / /
chen las kyi rdo rje'i sku gdung ril por bzhugs pa'i mchod rten mjal bar phebs te /

mkha' yas sprin dkar po 'khrigs pa'i dbus su /

g.yon du rgyal ba btsong kha pa bzhugs pa zhig gsal bar gzigs /
mi 'khrugs pa'i smon lam thugs rtsom gnang /

de dag gi dus nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa dang /

nam steng sogs su rim gyis phebs /

de nas smra bo lcog tu phebs /

sar bsam yas nas gnod sbyin chen po sku khog dang bcas te byon /

bsam las kyi phyogs la lag 'jog byas pa'i stabs kyis de ras rgyal ngos /
'bras spungs dge bshes /
don grub rgyal po'i spral ba la gri tshal tsam rgyab e chog gsung bar mi 'gab tshul gnang 'dug kyang ring por ma lon par sde ba gshegs 'dug /
sa ka zla ba'i nang du nang so rgya ri ba dpon blon gyis gdan drangs /
yar lam bad chen du dgongs rdzogs kyi gral dbu gnang /

sde dgon mtha' dag gi re ba yongs su bskab ste /
chos 'khor rgyal du phyags phebs /
tshes bcu bdun gyi gza' skar bzang ba dang bstun 'jigs byed kyi sgo nas zhugs 'bul mdzad /

chos 'khor rgyal gnyer gtad mdzad pas gtsang phyogs su 'phrin las rgyas pa dang khang pa phyogs su gdan 'dren 'byung pa'i spyan ltas shar /

chos skyong rnams la gnyer gtad mdzad pas /

rje btsun byams pa la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis bskor ba zhal gzigs /

pa sogs kyi bsu ba dang bcas seng ge rtse sde dgon gyis spyan drangs /
mgon po zhal gyi sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma bzang po bsnyes /
lhun po rtse chos sder phebs /

bla grang shar du bzhugs /
dge 'dun la mang ja 'gyed bcas /

mchod khang rnams su snyan dar spyan gzigs rgyas par gnang /
'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar bas thog drangs pa'i rten dang brten par bcas pa'i mchod khang ngo mtshar gyi bkod pa rgya chen po rnams mjal /
khyad par lo chen rin cen bzang pos 'phags yul nas gdan drangs pa'i bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi drung du mchod gtor spyan gzigs gya nom pa phul /
'phrin las gnyer gtang mdzad pas /
snyan dar rang bab tu byung ba dngos grub kyi mtshan mar 'dug /
phyag mtshan thong pa'i nang nas phud cig phyag tu dmod nas kyi tshul du bzhes pas /
de'i khrod du gser rdog po la ring bsrel yung 'bru lta bu gnyis tsam 'byar ba zhig byung /
der gur mgon dngos su zhal gzigs /
bse 'bag de shin tu gnyan pa'i stabs kyis /
gdung brgyud zhal ngo rnams dang gzhan nus mthu can 'ga' zhig ma gtogs /
gzhan gyis reg mi nus shing /
gal por reg na mi shis pa zhig 'ong gi yod 'dug kyang /
rje 'di nyid kyis zhal ras kyi rdul 'phyi ba sogs mdzad /
bse 'bag gi 'dra bshus ri mor bkod pa gnang /
thos bsam gling pa'i slob dpon de rmi lam gsal po yod 'dug par /
shel dkar du phebs lam cung zad gnyid du song tsan /
mi nag po 'jigs su rung ba gnyis byung bar su yin dris pas /
bse 'bag lcam bral yin phyag phyir 'gor zer /
de ni rin po che bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bas mi gyangs par kha'u brag rdzong pa'i snyan brgyud thun mong ma yin pa'i chos 'ga' rnams 'bul ba'i rtags su mngon /
lha khang chen pos brog drangs pa'i mchod khang gzims phug tshun chad kyang mjal bar mjad /
phebs pa la mngon du phyogs pa na phag gru'i phug pa'i sgrub chu 'phel zhing /
phug pa'i nang du phebs pa dang chu glo bur du lud pa byung /
gzhan yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltas shin tu mang ba byung bar brten /
der 'khod pa'i skye bo mtha' dag rje btsun brtse chen snying po'i zhabs kyi rnam par sprul pa'o zhes dad pa'i spu long g.yo bar gyur to / /
de nas kha'u skye lhas su phebs /
gnas 'di ni bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po nan tar thugs gtsigs che bas sru ram rang bzhin gyis 'du ba dang khyad par mtshar lugs pa zhes bstan pa'i snying po 'di nyid kyi 'byung ba'i gnas yin pa dang /
lhag par mgon po zhal rdo la dngos su thim pa yin 'dug pa nas /
dad mos chen pos rje mtshar chen gyi bla ma mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug kun spangs rdo ring pas phyag len bstan ba'i mgon khang chos skyong dngos bzhugs pa der /
bsgang sgo bsnyen sgrub mdod bcol sogs /
'phrin las rgyas par bcol /
dar yang snyan dar rang bab tu byung ba sogs 'phrin las sgrub pa'i mtshan ma khyad par can gzigs /
nam mkha' la 'ja' sprin rma bya'i gdugs phub pa ltar phyur @# / /
pas kun ya mtshan par 'dzin /
gcen lung bas thog drangs pa'i ska ser grangs med pa mjal bar 'ongs ba don dang ldan par mdzad /
rim gyis bo dong e'i gnas gzigs gnang /
dpal ldan a phyi mar mchod gtor spyan gzigs phul /
rje gong ma gnyis kyi thugs dam 'dzugs gtor brje ba gnang /
gzigs snang khyad par can byung lung nag shel dgar du nang sos thog drangs pa'i skya ser rnams la chos kyi bdud rtsi stsal /
slar gangs can chos 'phel dang bkra shis lhun po brgyud zha lu ri phug tu /
thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che'i sku dang nA ro'i bum chu sogs nang rten mtha' dag mjal ba gnang /
las kyi gshin rje dang /
lha mo rdo rje rab brtan mas 'phrin las bsgrubs par khas blangs /
de nas 'brong rtse chos sder phebs sde dgon gyis bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa zhus /
sngar 'breng rtse chos rjes phyag drug pa'i sku bzhengs rtsis la gsal kha med par mgon po bzhengs gsungs pas /
bzo bos mgon po zer na gur las 'os med snyam bzhengs pa'i gur mgon gyi sku 'dra /
mtshar lugs kyi snyan brgyud khyad 'phags rnams khyi 'byung khungs /
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi gcen rgya gar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis phyag nas mdzad pa'i byin rlabs can de mjal ba gnang /
ba snam lhun grub rtse dang /
'brong rtse /
rgal byed tshal du 'brug pa sprul sku ngag dbang nor bus gdan drangs /
dpon slob gnyis ka phan tshun du dag snang che bas phyag rtse sprod dang bcas te mjal /
khong rang gi phyag bzo'i rgya mtsho lpu ba las grub pa'i gnas pa lca de yang phyag tu bul /
rten mjal rnams zhib par gnang /
sprul sku ngag dbang nor bu 'di bka' rgyud pa'i bla ma /
sgom chen pa'i sbag sbug gi nyams med par /
dpon slob gnyis lugs zung gi gsung gleng zhib tu byung 'dug pas /
de nas bzung ste dge 'brug gnyis lugs legs kyi khul du byed par gda' /
de yang 'brug pa sprul ba'i skus de skabs dangs dangs dod dod mdzad 'dug kyang /
rjes su dpal sder sgar ba dang mdzal skabs dgas mngal sgar par bkur bzos 'bul phul ches pa'i gnas tshul gsan pas /
'bras spungs sprul skus de 'dra mdzad yod ma bsam /
de ltar na nged kyis kyang ma mjal na'ang yod pa 'dug ces thugs cung ma rengs skad /
'brug pa sprul sku 'di gsang sngags gsar rnying mdo tha snyad rig ba sogs la mkhas pa cam du ma zad /
dgos mi dgos kyi sa mtshams phyed cing ltag tshugs zin pa /
'jig rten phyogs nas kyang dgra go gnyen go tshang mchod pa zhig yin par snang /
de nas rtse chen du phebs /
dpon drung blo bde bas bsnyen bkur bteg /
rim gyis dpal 'khor bde chen du /
rta pa'i bsu ba nyis brgya skor dang /
dge 'dun pa stong ra can tsam gyi ser sbrengs dang bcas pas mdun bdar te phebs /
dge lugs pa'i grwa tshang bdun gyis nyin re bzhin 'bul ba bzang 'gran byas pa mchod rten dang gtsug lag khang 'khor ba tsam dang /
sa zhal gyi grwa tshang rnams kyis kyang bsnyen bkur zhing /
rdo gcal du skya ser gyi tshogs la bka' gdams glegs bam dang /
'du khang du tshogs pa la snar thang brgya rtsa /
gzims chung dus dge ris med la gur zhal gyi rjes gnang dang /
rab byung bsnyen rdzogs gnang /
mchod rten chen mo /
gos sku mchod khang rnams mjal zhing bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam mdzad /
rgyal mkhar cher nang chen pas gdan drangs /
gus mchod bla ltag tu bsgrubs /
de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung cha brgyad du bgos pa'i rgyal bo ma skyes @# / /
dgra'i rten skal gyi 'phel gdung /

ring bsrel gcig gnyis shig 'bul rtsis la smon lam gnang bas bco lnga rang bab tu phyag tu byung /

ri khrod dga' ldan du gdan drangs /
gnas de'i spod ba bsam gtan pa'i dge 'dun rnams la chos kyi 'brel ba stsal /
rgya sngags 'chang chen bo mjal /
dpal gsang ba'i gdung 'dzin gnas rnying chos rjes lha mgon lcam bral gyi 'cham sku sogs bsu ba'i bkod pa dang bcas te gdan drangs /
gser 'bum dang khyad 'phags bcu gsum sogs gnas gzigs zhib par gnang /
zhal ngo grwa bu slob rnams la 'dod chos stsal zhing zhabs tog kyang rgya cher mdzad /
khyad par zhabs drung chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung ya mtshan can zhig phul /
stong sher 'brog pa rnams kyi khrod du gdan drangs te yig drug gi bzlas lung dang bsnyen gnas sogs dge ba'i lam la bkod /
phyir lam dpon drung rtse bas dbang ldan chos 'khor du bsnyen bkur zhus| slar gnas rnying du phebs te mkhan pos thog drangs pa'i der 'khod thams cad la chos dang zang zing gi dga' ston stsal /
rab byung bsnyen rdzogs brgya skor bsgrubs /

thams cad mkhyen pa ni /

sku mdun chos bzang 'phrin las gnyis kyis skor g.yang byas pas /

de yang rje bsod nams rgya mtsho de thugs dag snang che bas /

dbang rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos du ma stsal /
gser dngul gis dar rta phyags sogs 'bul ba khri phrag brgal ba phul /
sa skyong zhes pa shing bya'i lo gsar dang /
cho 'phrul gyi mchod pa rgyas par mdzad /
rab tu byung ba stong phrag nye ba bsgrubs /
gtsug lag khang dang 'dus pa'i sde gsar du bskrun pa la me tog gtor /
da yan no yon de sdig la rngams shing mi bsrun pa srin po'i rigs can lta bu zhig yin 'dug kyang /
yan lag brgyad pa'i bslab pa la bkod de sdig la shin tu 'dzam par gyur /
de nas se chen ta'i ching gi sde thog tu bzhugs sgar phebs /
tha'i ji la tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du bcug ste dbang bskur /
gtsug lag khang dang 'dus sde bzhengs pa la rab tu gnas pa dang /
gshin rje gshed kyi drag po'i sbyin sreg gis nag phyogs rnams tshar bcad /
dgon pa de la phun tshogs dar rgyas gling du btags /
than pa shin tu che ba la char chen po phab ste mi phyugs mtha' dag bde ba la bkod /

'di dag gi skabs snga phyi rnams su phyag mdud phyag dbang sogs grangs mang bas phyag brdol ba byung yang 'gro don la dgongs te dkris ma mdzad nas mtshams 'jog pa ma gnang /

yig cha kha yar 'dug pa rnams la gzhi byas /
sprul sku 'phrang kha bas mdzad ba de nyid la lo tshigs sogs shin tu ngag par 'dug cing /
gzhan rnams la snga phyi'i lo dus 'dzol ba dang /
brjod don 'phyugs pa kha yar mchis na'ang /
lo tshigs nor ba sogs ma dag pa rnams la zhib mor dbyad /
rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po 'khon ston chos kyi rgyal po dpal 'byor lhun grub sogs yongs 'dzin dam pa chos bzhin du sbyod pa du ma'i gsung ngag las ji ltar thos pa rnams dang /
gzhan yang skad gnyis smra ba zhang mkhar lotsA ba 'jam dpal rdo rje sogs mang du thos pa'i yon tan mkhan po mang po'i ngag rgyun khungs btsun gyi rigs kyis zur brgyan /
bar skabs kyi tshigs bcad rnams ma gtogs kun gyi go bde ba'i phyir 'bol rtsom du byas te /
lo rgyus smra ba'i btsun ba ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho 'jigs med go cha thub bstan lang tsho'i sdes| mi zad pa me pho phyi'i lo /
nyin mor byed pa srang gi khyim du spyod pa'i phyogs gnyis ba'i rgyal ba gsum ba'i tshes la dga' ldan pho brang du sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni ngag dbang dge legs so / /
